Arrangements with Named Executive Officers Change Control Arrangements\x97Stock Options, Restricted Stock, and Restricted Stock Units the event "change control" the Company, all outstanding options under the Company\' stock option plans, except the Director Plan, will, unless otherwise determined the plan administrator, become exercisable full, and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price. The Director Plan provides that upon "change control" the Company, all unvested options held non-employee directors will automatically become fully vested and exercisable and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price the options. "change control" under these plans generally defined ( ) the acquisition any person % more the combined voting power the Company\' outstanding securities ( ) the occurrence transaction requiring shareholder approval and involving the sale all substantially all the assets the Company the merger the Company with into another corporation. addition, options, restricted stock grants, and restricted stock units granted the Named Executive Officers generally provide that the event there "change control," defined the Company\' stock option plans, and connection with following such "change control," their employment terminated without "Cause" they should resign for "Good Reason," those options, restricted stock, and restricted stock units outstanding that are not yet vested the date such "change control" shall become fully vested. Further, restricted stock and restricted stock units granted the Named Executive Officers also provide that, the event the Company terminates the Officer without cause any time, the restricted stock units and restricted stock will vest full. Generally, "Cause" defined include felony conviction, willful disclosure confidential information willful and continued failure perform his her employment duties. "Good Reason" includes resignation employment result substantial diminution position duties, adverse change title reduction annual base salary. Item . Policy Audit Committee Pre-Approval Audit and Non-Audit Services Performed the Independent Registered Public Accounting Firm Prior the enactment the Sarbanes-Oxley Act (the " Act "), the Company adopted auditor independence policy that banned its auditors from performing non-financial consulting services, such information technology consulting and internal audit services. This auditor policy also mandates that the audit and non-audit services and the related budget approved the Audit Committee advance, and that the Audit Committee provided with quarterly reporting actual spending. This policy also mandates that auditor engagements for non-audit services may entered into without the express approval the Audit Committee. Role the Board; Corporate Governance Matters the paramount duty the Board Directors oversee the Chief Executive Officer and other senior management the competent and ethical operation the Company day- -day basis and assure that the long-term interests the shareholders are being served. satisfy this duty, the directors take proactive, focused approach their position, and set standards ensure that the Company committed business success through maintenance the highest standards responsibility and ethics. Members the Board bring the Company wide range experience, knowledge and judgment. These varied skills mean that good governance depends far more than "check the box" approach standards procedures. The governance structure the Company designed working structure for principled actions, effective decision-making and appropriate monitoring both compliance and performance. The key practices and procedures the Board are outlined the Corporate Governance Guidelines available the Company\' website www apple com investor. Board Committees The Board has standing Compensation Committee, Nominating and Corporate Governance Committee (" Nominating Committee" ) and Audit and Finance Committee (" Audit Committee "). The Compensation Committee primarily responsible for reviewing the compensation arrangements for the Company\' executive officers, including the Chief Executive Officer, and for administering the Company\' stock option plans. Members the Compensation Committee are Messrs. Campbell, Drexler and Gore. The Nominating Committee assists the Board identifying qualified individuals become directors, determines the composition the Board and its committees, monitors the process assess Board effectiveness and helps develop and implement the Company\' corporate governance guidelines. Members the Nominating Committee are Messrs. Drexler and Gore and . Levinson. The Audit Committee primarily responsible for overseeing the services performed the Company\' independent auditors and internal audit department, evaluating the Company\' accounting policies and its system internal controls and reviewing significant financial transactions. Members the Audit Committee are Messrs. Campbell and York and . Levinson. The Audit, Compensation and Nominating Committees operate under written charters adopted the Board. These charters are available the Company\' website www apple com investor. The current practice the Board base substantial portion director\' annual retainer equity. , shareholders approved the Director Stock Option Plan (the " Director Plan" ) and , shares were reserved for issuance thereunder. Pursuant the Director Plan, the Company\' non-employee directors are granted option acquire , shares Common Stock upon their initial election the Board (" Initial Options" ). The Initial Options vest and become exercisable three equal annual installments each the first through third anniversaries the grant date. the fourth anniversary non-employee director\' initial election the Board and each subsequent anniversary thereafter, the director will entitled receive option acquire , shares Common Stock (" Annual Options" ). Annual Options are fully vested and immediately exercisable their date grant. the end the fiscal year, there were options for , shares outstanding under the Director Plan. Non-employee directors also receive $ , annual retainer paid quarterly increments. addition, directors receive two free computer systems per year and are eligible purchase additional equipment discount. Directors not receive any additional consideration for serving committees committee chairperson. Arrangements with Named Executive Officers Change Control Arrangements\x97Stock Options, Restricted Stock, and Restricted Stock Units the event "change control" the Company, all outstanding options under the Company\' stock option plans, except the Director Plan, will, unless otherwise determined the plan administrator, become exercisable full, and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price. The Director Plan provides that upon "change control" the Company, all unvested options held non-employee directors will automatically become fully vested and exercisable and will cashed out amount equal the difference between the applicable "change control price" and the exercise price the options. "change control" under these plans generally defined ( ) the acquisition any person % more the combined voting power the Company\' outstanding securities ( ) the occurrence transaction requiring shareholder approval and involving the sale all substantially all the assets the Company the merger the Company with into another corporation. addition, options, restricted stock grants, and restricted stock units granted the Named Executive Officers generally provide that the event there "change control," defined the Company\' stock option plans, and connection with following such "change control," their employment terminated without "Cause" they should resign for "Good Reason," those options, restricted stock, and restricted stock units outstanding that are not yet vested the date such "change control" shall become fully vested. Further, restricted stock and restricted stock units granted the Named Executive Officers also provide that, the event the Company terminates the Officer without cause any time, the restricted stock units and restricted stock will vest full. Generally, "Cause" defined include felony conviction, willful disclosure confidential information willful and continued failure perform his her employment duties. Policy Audit Committee Pre-Approval Audit and Non-Audit Services Performed the Independent Registered Public Accounting Firm Prior the enactment the Sarbanes-Oxley Act (the " Act "), the Company adopted auditor independence policy that banned its auditors from performing non-financial consulting services, such information technology consulting and internal audit services. This auditor policy also mandates that the audit and non-audit services and the related budget approved the Audit Committee advance, and that the Audit Committee provided with quarterly reporting actual spending. This policy also mandates that auditor engagements for non-audit services may entered into without the express approval the Audit Committee.
